< Name>

<date>1525899602696<//date><rating>5</rating><Review>Just driving by the filling station, you probably wouldn't realize it's a coffee stand. Their brewed coffee is pretty good, better than Starbucks I'd say. The specialty lattes are tasty too - and there are so many flavors and combos to choose from! My favorites are the Mexican Mocha and Kahlua White Russian (hot, not blended). Their iced teas are great too! I haven't tried many but peachy beachy is yummy!

If there is already a line of cars waiting, it's easy to get impatient. <Rating>3< /Rating><text>2.5 STARS -

I have always wanted to give this place a try.  It looks so neat and cool when you pass it as you drive by so today I decided to go ahead and follow my gut.  The menu looked very interesting and delicious. Now as I drive up the female barista is chatting with the patron ahead of me...that's no problem I figure maybe she just placed her order and is waiting for her goods.   5 minutes go by...then 10 minutes go by.  I notice that the barista hasn't left the window.  Her elbow is propped up in the window and the 2 women are just shooting the breeze.  more than enough time has passed and the car ahead of me should have gotten her order by now...but no.  by this time cars pull up to the opposite window( and are waiting) and a walk up order was made and  completed.  when the car in front of me gets her order...it is 4 drinks and nothing else!   I finally pull up to the window.  The female barista looks at me a number of times but never comes to the window.  She could have easily said, "I'll  be right with you" or "It'll be a few more minutes, if you don't mind the wait" but do you think she did that?  after another 3-5 minutes of sitting at the window she indicates to the male barista to come to the window and with a friendly greeting he takes my order (a 12oz hot ambrosia latte). a very short time later he returns with my drink ready to hand to me and a smile on his face.  If it had not been for the 2nd barista I guarantee that today would've been my last time visiting the Filling station.  The drink was very good but the customer service (initially) was unprofessional. I do plan on giving it another try and I can only hope that I don't receive the same service I received today.< /text>< time>

< text>
Very satisfied customer! I live about an hour away from this Maaco but made the drive to have David look at my car that was in desperate need of restoration. I went to several other body shops near me (including other Maaco stores)- some cheaper, some way more money.. In the end I chose David and his team at Maaco Fremont because he is a man of his word and the quality of their work is best in class. The entire team I dealt with was friendly and happy to interact with me. Upon first arriving, David wanted to know what I wanted out of this paint job before making recommendations. He took diligent notes and then walked me through his shop to show me several different stages of paint and quality of work- PRIDE of workmanship! I am very OCD in general, and even more about my car. His attention to detail and general positive attitude was a blessing. He gave me a fair price and realistic timeline for the project. He kept me informed throughout the project as I was over an hour away and couldn't come see it at will. The paint job turned out PHENOMENAL. They even replaced metal where rust formed in fenders and bumper area- AND they did it the right way. It looks incredible and no concerns of rust coming back. The paint job looks better than new as I elected for the premium base/clear and polish on my car. Zero orange peel and very glossy look to it. Overall it was a 10/10 paint job and 10/10 experience. I would absolutely recommend this Maaco- If you are within 2 hours drive... Go see David and his team. You won't regret it. Picking the right place is key to getting the right results!< /text>

< review>
I have a 1960 Jaguar classic car which I am restoring on a budget. Great hobby!

It needed a full paintjob, and a bit of body work here and there. I would not take it to any Maaco, but after having seen the reviews for David Gutierrez and his team in South Fremont, I decided to hand over my jewel in their care.

And boy, did they do a good job!

From the time I walked through the door, to when I picked it up again, I was treated with respect and professionalism. I was walked through the process and what to expect in great detail, and I was invited to visit as much as I wanted to follow the progress of the project.

There were a few body work items that they were not sure they were able to handle. That was made clear to me from the beginning, but they actually were successful in manufacturing the parts in good quality.

The paint job is wonderful. They helped me chose the exact, era-correct colors, which must have taken some time. Their prep work was impeccable (thanks Mike!), so the final product came out perfect.

The total price for the whole thing came in a bit lower than originally quoted, which of course doesn‚Äôt' hurt.

Please support this fine businessman and his team. You will not regret it.< /review>

< review>
Pros:
* Good service, quick, courteous and friendly.
* Car was clean and modern with full tank and everything working quite well. It was an Eco drive as well so it was good on our gas budget.
* They have a variety of cars to chose and they'll suggest a car based on your needs and travelling requirements.
* Flexible schedule. They're open from 8 to 8 and if you need anything just give them a call.
* Not the cheapest ever, but competitive prices.
* They informed us about some promotions they have that helped with our interests. They weren't focused or ripping us off. They really wanted to help and find the best option for our needs.
* No age fee. You can be under 25 and drive as long as you have a driver's license and credit card.

Cons:
*It's a small place quite hidden. We got a bit lost finding the place.
*You can't drive outside California.

I'd definitely recommend this place to anyone who needs a car.</review>

<userid>103264931057315660633< /userid><user_name>Chris Yerkes<//user_name><Time>1490768039360< /Time><Rating>1< /Rating>< review>
Can't say how disappointed I was in the service and the food we received on the night of 3/25/2017.

Upon entering the restaurant, my wife and I were the first out of a party of 4 to get there. We stood around waiting for someone to seat us and was rather annoyed that out of the 3 servers and the one bartender, we were being unnoticed. I eventually had to walk up to a server and ask if anyone was going to seat us. Mind you, the establishment was not overly busy at the time. Strike one.

A few minutes later, our other two guests arrived.  Our server gave us some waters and had us look over the menu. One of our guests asks the server if she could sample a beer. It was super awkward when the sever questioned the sampling of a beer. There was a moment of pause and a bewildered look to the servers face.  It couldn't be more obvious that the server was shocked that someone wanted a sample of a beer.  I wanted a lighter beer and a Pacifico sounded good. The server came back and told me that they were out of Pacifico. Who runs out of Pacifico?  Really?  Strike two.

Upon ordering our dinner, the server fesses up that it's her second day on the job and that this restaurant is different than her last. Okay, I get it, I understand. I've worked in a restaurant before and I know how hectic it can be.  This note is for the manager there, if there is one. If you have a new server who doesn't seem like they know what they are doing, perhaps it would behoove you to have your other employees help them out. It would make your patron's experience much better, and perhaps would make your employees much happier in the long run.  So we order our food and my wife decides on the short rib. The server then asks how does she want it cooked?  Is that a trick question?  No, she was serious.  We finally get our food and everyone's dinner looks okay with the exception of my wife's short rib. It came out grey, super dry, and lacking of all flavor. We send it back and order their grilled cheese. Literally it takes them almost 20 minutes to make it and they forgot the bacon. Whatever at this point. Strike three.

Lastly, please ensure the restrooms have an adequate supply of paper towels.

Go at your own risk.< /review>

<rating>4</rating><user_id>105692744256480109238<//user_id>< Review>
Duck Fat Fried Chicken and Waffles ($17) is served with maple butter and crow hot sauce. The exterior is golden brown and crispy. The duck fat flavor is definitely apparent and adds a richness to the chicken. The chicken is tender and juicy. The waffle is pretty good, but adding the maple butter and syrup makes it a winner. The hot sauce gives it a spicy kick to get you going on a Sunday morning. Rating: 4.8/5

The Crow "Black Label" Burger ($19) is an 8 oz. signature blend beef patty (including 21 day dry aged prime ribeye) served on a brioche bun with bone marrow butter, and caramelized onions. The burger patty is juicy and meaty. The bone marrow butter adds a creamy richness to the burger and caramelized onions add sweetness. The brioche bun is soft yet sturdy and holds the juices in the burger. Add a side of duck fat fries. The fries have a crispy exterior and kettle chip flavor with a soft, fluffy interior. Rating: 4.8/5

"Smores" ($10) is a graham cracker cake topped with milk chocolate and toasted marshmallow ice cream. The cake has a solid texture, almost like cornbread. It has an in-your-face graham cracker flavor. The marshmallow ice cream is creamy, fluffy, and tastes like ice cold marshmallow cr√®me. Hershey's chocolate mini bars are at room temperature so it is slightly soft for a melt-in-your-mouth s'mores experience. All that is missing is a little bit of burned sugar! Rating: 3.5/5< /Review>

I needed to get a RealID as my license was expiring in December but I was always put off by the huge perpetual lines wrapping around the building. <Rate>5<//Rate><review>In the middle of this pandemic, I was required to renew my license in person because it had been renewed automatically by mail the past two times. I was so worried about having to go to the DMV office during this COVID-19 pandemic. I fully expected a horrible experience, but it was very easy and pleasant! Seriously-- they have developed a nice and efficient system for getting everyone through, in-and-out quickly. I arrived early, about 30 minutes before opening time, and there were about 20 people already in line outside. But a DMV employee (a perfectly professional and knowledgeable gentleman with long brown/gray hair like mine) came outside and went down the line, helping every person in the line to organize their documents and provide their confirmation code, if applicable, and giving each of us our call number for our turn inside the DMV. Inside the office, all employees were wearing face shields and chairs were 6 feet apart. Customers were allowed to enter only to fill the available widely-spaced chairs.
The process was completed very efficiently and the entire office seemed safe¬†and orderly. The personnel were very nice and professional.<//review>< resp>

< Text>
IT IS WHAT IT IS ! My wife and I have been itching to get our REAL ID's taken care of for some time but the covid lockdown blew that plan out of the water until Monday. My diligent and smart wife took care of the fine application details online so we just had to front up in person without an appointment ( because thems are the rules ). Of course we all know how long the lines can get at the DMV. We left home at 10am to hopefully beat the rush or simply give us time to burn for a long wait in line. When we pulled into the carpark at 10.30am I nearly had cardiac arrest when I saw the long line waiting OUTSIDE the building. Remember there is already a stack of people waiting inside to be processed. We tried to find where the line started...the right line for the purpose of our visit. There were 3 different lines....a short one for driver's license tests, a really big line for everything and another short line for whatever. My wife had told me that because we had our paperwork completed already that we would get priority. There was no way to tell how we would get that priority until a smallish DMV female employee worked her way along the big line and took our temps, asked us a couple of questions and then gave us a couple of DMV Screened stickers to display on our clothing. A little while later we found out we did have priority and the same smallish and helpful female DMV employee led us inside the DMV building. We were left in front of a desk to be interviewed by another female DMV employee. Gee things were moving along briskly ! After waiting a few minutes for our allotted numbers to be called out ( and displayed simultaneously on an overhead monitor ) we were both individually photographed and told our new REAL ID Licenses would arrive in about 3 weeks. We were impressed !< /Text>
